| <span data-ttu-id="dbd73-695">進入</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dbd73-695">Entry</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="dbd73-696">值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dbd73-696">Value</span></span> |
